function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

if (!is_file('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_example_data_sqlite');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_example_data_sqlite');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite') != 'e963c71a1af7416e6488491aa79b29d373079beb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_example_data_sqlite');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_example_data_sqlite');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite') !== 'e963c71a1af7416e6488491aa79b29d373079beb') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite') !== 'ac8e213a1af51b6cd8ce530747a6311e8d526117') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_example_data_sqlite');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_example_data_sqlite') !== 'e963c71a1af7416e6488491aa79b29d373079beb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_example_data_sqlite');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') != '2c48c9cc0815be4f93dbd525f9aa4d6a851b2587') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '2c48c9cc0815be4f93dbd525f9aa4d6a851b2587') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '94a0d86e98b1b2e6ad35427a0daa1dfa4a7b917d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '2c48c9cc0815be4f93dbd525f9aa4d6a851b2587') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
}
